The Path of Public and Private Affairs
Everyone knows that in human society, we cannot live beyond history. When we talk about 'historicity,' it includes the past, present, and future. If what I am saying now is the present, then what I just said is already the past, and what I will say next becomes the future. This means that our human life, or human existence, begins in this kind of relationship. 
Every human being desires to be a being with a broad and vast historicity. 
When we look at it, we see that three points are connected. Some people emphasize the past, some emphasize the present, and some emphasize the future. 
If you are an American citizen, you take pride in the present, but you also take pride in the past and the future. So, when we look at the country of America, is it a country that is becoming greater and greater, or is it a country that was great in the past, is small in the present, and will become even smaller in the future? (While writing on the board) Which is it? Is it the first or the second? "It is the first." 
Now, when we look at this, there is a path of public and private affairs, and we need to discern whether America is leaning toward the public or the private. The public refers to the larger, while the private refers to the smaller. Isn't that right? The public speaks of the larger. 
What does it mean to be large? What content does it refer to when we say it is large right now, and what content does it refer to when we say it is small? For example, if we take Mark as an individual, he is just one person, but what is large and what is small? When we look at one person, we can say there is a public person and a private person. There is a public Mark and a private Mark. We say, "Ah, that person is a great person," and also, "That person is a petty person." When we say something is great, we refer to the future. We need to have the concept that greatness refers to the future. If we say the present is great, then there is no future. 
Now, when we look at the history of humanity, among humanity, what kind of background do those who have contributed to creating cultural spheres and the human world have? They have a foundation that has worked centered on the future and over a long period of time to contribute to the establishment of the cultural world. That is a fact. 
What is that background? We can understand that the religious concept has contributed much more to the historical world than the concept of the nation. Therefore, we must always recognize that the stronger and larger the solid concept of a nation or religion regarding the future, the more that nation or religion will develop. It develops because there is effort put into it. 
Now, when we center on the present, everything splits into two paths. The past was great, and the future is in opposition. If this has become so large, then this becomes like this, and this becomes an X-ray. (While writing on the board) This is how it is; the present is like this. Our human history weaves these things together. 
Then what is human desire? "Ah! I wish I had been this great in the past. I hope I can be this great in the future." We cannot help but think this way. Originally, if everything from the past through the present to the future had been ideal like a log, how wonderful would that be? This is the thought that arises. Now, the question arises. What do we desire? Everyone wants this. (While pointing to what was written) 
There is a three-world concept that summarizes all of this in history: one where the past is great and the future is small, one where the future is great and the past is small, and then one where everything is great. We can extract these three from any field of human historical periods. Some might say, "Oh, I am not like that." However, you all want to have not just one friend but many. This is the nature of human desire. Humans inherently seek to establish broad relationships and connections. Isn't that right? "Yes." 
Countries like China, despite having nothing, boast about having "one billion people!" What does that mean? It means they desire to be broad, to be vast. What does that mindset imply? Ultimately, it indicates a longing for a broad historicity. 
For God, humanity, and the future, a person who lives for the public is a public person. 
So, if God exists, what do you think God would think? Which of these three would He choose? "The third." That is what He would choose. It is a fact. If God is like that, then why has such a world not come to be, despite His omnipotence? That is the question. Why has it not happened? 
God is a public being. He is a public God, so why has it not happened? Would He have created Adam and Eve and then intended to shrink from there, or to expand? "To expand." Expansion, indeed. From there, a woman stands for a man, a man stands for a woman, parents stand for children, children stand for families, families stand for tribes, tribes stand for nations, and nations stand for states, gradually becoming greater. (While writing on the board) God created this world and the invisible world. We are the mediators of both worlds. When this is established, ultimately, this comes to be. If this becomes like this, then this actually comes to be. It is a thought that comes to existence. (While pointing to what was written) We cannot help but think that God had some purpose to align humanity with this kind of concept. He hoped that this would become this and that would become that. (While pointing to what was written) Do you understand? 
But what happened to humanity? They did not think of becoming greater; they denied the great being and chose a path that would make everything smaller in the future. This world is a world of death, and this world is a world of life. This is the world of God, and this is the world of Satan. Now, what is the fall of the human world? Humans must stand in the position of serving the public God and standing for the future. We must recognize that this is the public position. God is not in the past. Therefore, we can find that we must become people who serve the past and the future. Ultimately, what does this mean? It means that a public person is one who lives for God, for future descendants, and for future nations. 
So, what was God like? After creating Adam and Eve, when God was with Adam and Eve, would He have said, "Hey, you, Eve, and you, Adam, don't think about yourselves or your children; just think about me"? "No." He would have said, "Think of Adam and Eve as you think of me." That is the kind of education He would have given. That is all we can say. If He said, "Love only me," then there would be no past for God. It would also deny the present and the past. Isn't that so? "Yes." 
That is why God would have said to Adam, "Hey! You love me, right? You like me?" If Adam said, "Yes," God would have said, "You should love Eve more than you love me." He would have undoubtedly said that. This indicates that He provided good education. We must recognize that God Himself had a concept of the future. There is no other way. Therefore, we must live for tomorrow more than today, for the day after tomorrow more than tomorrow, and for the next year more than this year. 
That is why there is a distinction between retreating from the present and advancing. Retreating from the present leads to hell, while advancing leads to heaven. Is heaven in the present or in the future? Because of the fall, where is it? Is it in the present or in the future? "In the future." It is not in the present. Heaven is not in the present; it is in the future. 
Now, our Unification Church is working for the will of God. As a member of the Unification Church, where does a person who retreats go? They are falling. They are heading toward hell. Is that correct? "Yes." The present is difficult; it is hard to live. What should we do? Should we retreat? "No." Then what should we do? "We should advance." 
If we look at everything comprehensively, it becomes simple. If God exists, when He educates Adam, He would say, "Hey! You two, Adam and Eve, love each other. Love each other more than you love me!" That is the kind of education He would have provided. Therefore, we conclude that we must establish the principle of loving more than ourselves. If Reverend Moon is a public leader, when he speaks, he would not say, "Oh, if you love me, do not love the future more than me." That is a leader who is heading toward Satan's side. That is the conclusion. That is ultimately heading toward Satan. That is self-centered. It is centered around oneself. This gives rise to the concept of being self-centered. Ultimately, this leads to retreating. There is no future. 
Hell means there is no future. Heaven has a future; hell has no future. Even if you enter heaven, there is a future. We must understand this. 
The public seeks something greater than oneself, while the private seeks something smaller than oneself, desiring to retreat. They do not think about the future. They cannot think about the future. They only think about the present and the past. Do you understand? "Yes." 
Where does the fall originate? The fall begins from a position that lacks the public meaning of the future, from a place centered only on oneself. You must understand this. Do you understand? The path that serves oneself leads to hell, while the path that serves others leads to heaven. This concept is established. 
To be a nation is to be in the present. It is connected from the past to the present. To be another is to be in the future. It is relative. Being relative means it is the next stage of oneself. What does that mean? When God spoke to Adam, saying, "You! Love Eve more than you love me," it meant to think greater than the present. Do you clearly understand this? "Yes." 
Therefore, the Unification Church teaches us to live for others. The conclusion is that we should live for others. When I am alone, I live for myself, but when there is a counterpart, I should value and love the counterpart more than myself. Parents should value their children more. This is the stage we have reached. And families should value society more. We can find this concept in the perspective that families should love tribes more, tribes should love nations more, nations should love the world more, and the world should love heaven and earth more. We have discovered that this concept is continuous. 
Loving and sacrificing for something greater is the principle of justice. 
Now, if we center on the duality, the positive and negative revolve, right? (While writing on the board) "Yes." Why do they revolve like this? Why are they both rotating? To create the world, to create the universe.... If the positive says, "Hmm, I must be smaller than you; do not be great," the universe will not come into being. Therefore, these two must unite and say, "Let us revolve around something that loves us more than ourselves," so that the universe can form. The great universe is formed. Do you understand? 
Our Unification Church members say, "Individuals live for families, families live for tribes, tribes live for nations, nations live for the world, and the world lives for heaven and earth, for God!" What does that mean? It means to love each other. Love. The universe becomes one through love. This is the principle. We can grasp the concept that the universe is formed through love, through love that values and sacrifices for something greater. This is indeed true. There is no doubt about it. 
When there is a family, if that family values relatives or the whole neighborhood more than their own family, does the neighborhood not unite with that family? It is the same. Centered around that family, everyone should strive to value each other. If someone says, "Why should I care? Love me," then kick! The universe cannot exist there. The universe does not come into being. 
Therefore, you must understand that the small sacrifices for the greater are public. If you do not know this, it will be a big problem. That is public. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." When a cow grazes, is it private or public? From the perspective of the grass? "It is public." (Laughter) Then from the perspective of the cow? That is private. It is private, but if the cow says, "I eat this grass for the benefit of future humans, to respond 100 percent to humans," then that is public. Being eaten by humans is public from the perspective of the cow. For humans to eat the cow is private. However, when it says, "I eat for something greater," then it becomes public. 
Therefore, from the small to the large.... What is the public path? This means this is for this, this is for this, this is for this, and this is for this. This is the logic, isn't it? It is all public. Do you understand? Then, when I eat, it is private in itself. However, when I eat, I say, "I eat for something greater, to connect with something greater." 
Then the idea that the small is equal to the large is established.
When you look at it, you think, 'This form, this is all me. This is my extension!' This is the idea. If you think this way, it feels unpleasant, but if you think this way, how good does it feel? (Pointing to what he wrote on the board) 

Imagine if one cell of that grass could become God's flesh through a cow and a person, it could become blood, just one cell. Imagine if that cell became one that God could love. It has become a cell of God's body. When you think about that, would that grass cell be happy to give something else? As long as it receives God's love... Now, your beloved wives and husbands say, 'Oh, I love you more than money,' right? 'As long as there is love, that's enough,' they say, claiming they would die for love and live for love.

That is why in the Bible, Jesus says, 'Those who want to die will live, and those who want to live will die, and those who want to be high will be brought low, and those who want to be low will be lifted high...' What does that mean? It centers around love. Think about it: those who want to die centered on love will live, and those who want to live will die. How wonderful is that? Just think if you left this out. If a man died centered on such love, then based on the love of that deceased husband, a path for the wife to leap forward would arise. A path for leaping forward arises. History has developed like that. Do you understand what I mean? 「Yes」 You need to understand this clearly.

In countries like America today, this is a mess. It's chaotic. Among humanity, what is it? When you look at it this way, can the individualists who pride themselves in America establish a relationship with heaven and the future world? They cannot. That is why America will perish. It will become hell. To become hell is to perish.

What is different about our Unification Church? You need to know that. The reason I am saying this is that you will need to engage in intense activities from now on, but if you do not clearly understand the path of public and private, you will get exhausted. You will get tired. Therefore, when I ask you to sacrifice, it means to implant my cells here. It means to transplant cancer tissue, in the form of cancer cells. How much faster will that spread than cancer cells? (Laughter) Do you think it will be that way or not? 「I think so.」

The reason our Unification Church is not developing is that everyone is avoiding difficult tasks, dislikes hardships, and likes what is enjoyable. They say, 'I don't want to suffer.' Reverend Moon is busy sacrificing today and tomorrow, rather than thinking, 'I will succeed because I am doing well.' It may seem like nothing is happening, but behind the scenes, it is continuously growing. 'Oh, I will become like this. God will do this for me,' they think. If God does it, fine, and now that I know my path, I will go. Look. The individual exists for the family. The family exists for the tribe. Knowing that, I will go for the world until I reach that point for the individual. I will go. If God acknowledges it, fine, and if the world acknowledges it, fine, I will go. As I go, the world changes and resurrects. It is similar to what resurrects before God in the spirit world. Therefore, there is no need to think about such things.

When God becomes the center of the nation and comes to that nation, He will say to the president of that nation, 'Hey, you! You must go for the world! You must love more than the people of this nation!' Isn't that how it should be? 'As long as you think of your country, you cannot love the world!' Is that how it is? It is the same principle. What that means is that you should work hard for the greater stage in front of you. If you work hard, it will naturally arise in the spirit world; it does not arise because you are trying to do it. That is the principle of creation.

Home church is a place where you can live a life of service. 

In that sense, when the teacher says, 'Do home church,' it is public. 'Why do home church?' When someone makes excuses like, 'Oh! The newspaper company is busy, how can we do it two by two!' I would say, 'You just eat rice. Don't drink water.' What would happen? 'Oh! I need to eat water, and I need to eat other things; I must eat everything.' They will say that. They will say they will do this and that but refuse to do home church—that is not acceptable. That is wrong. We must all do it together. Just like eating water and rice, we must do it together. 'I rejoice more than eating rice or drinking water,' if that thought exists, it is enough.

So, you eat rice and drink water, but why do you eat? It is for home church. Therefore, you should have a heart that values home church more than eating rice and drinking water. If you do not have that heart, you cannot. You will fall away. If you are busy, you should at least go there and sleep. You should do it yourself. (Laughter) If you cannot work, you should at least look. If you love someone, you cannot just wander around for a year without visiting them and then come back saying, 'I was wrong!' You must at least go and see them once, even if you cannot show love... That is what I am saying.

Also, in home church, there are people waiting for you spiritually, and if you do not go, at that time, your blessings will be taken away. Those in home church live like they are trapped in a wire fence. They are banging on it, saying, 'I want to break free from this wire fence! Oh, oh!' They are making a fuss. Do you understand? (Drawing a picture while speaking. Laughter) They are asking to be freed, but they do not go and do not listen. If you cannot do that, you should at least pray. Even when you sit down to eat, you should say, 'Oh, God! I am sorry I cannot go to my home church.' If you do not do that and eat three meals, you guys! Then you say, 'Oh, the teacher taught me something good. He said I should pray, so I can just pray.' That will not work. (Laughter) If you pray, you must act. If you pray once, you must go and come back once. You should go and see them once. If not, you should at least go up the mountain and take a look and then pray. What will happen if you just pray every day?

Raise your hands if you attended the engagement ceremony this time. Did you think there is a fiancé in that home church? If there is, would you go there or not? You see them every day with your eyes... (Acting while speaking. Laughter) Is home church less than your fiancé? 「No」 You must sacrifice even with your fiancé. You must do home church even if it requires sacrifice.

Fiancés write letters, right? Should we not write letters for a year? Cut it all off. 'Oh! What a chatter...' But loving home church more than loving your wife has become the principle. That is not my word. It is a public word, a public statement.

As for the teacher, he destroyed his family for the sake of the will. It seems like a great sin, but it is not a sin. If I did it for myself, that would be a sin. But if I did it for the nation and the world, that is another matter. It is public. Do you understand? You are confused about this.

If you have become the teacher's wife, and the teacher says, 'Hey, let’s sacrifice together for the world!' you should say 'Yes' and follow. If you say, 'Oh, I don’t want to!' should I follow or abandon this? That is a sin. If you follow, you cannot be forgiven. That is a sin. You should say, 'Even if you go, I will not go.' If you had said, 'For my children, I will not center around myself...' would the Unification Church of today have come into existence? 「No, it would not have.」 It did not come into existence.

Now, if Reverend Moon sacrificed you from a public standpoint and instilled resentment in you, you might think it is private and feel guilty, but that is public.

How good would it have been if I had not fought with America? How good would it have been if I had not fought with Congress or President Carter? I am saying we should fight not for ourselves but for America, for the world, for heaven. Sacrificing myself... You need to understand that. I fought with the thought of risking my life and going to prison for the world and heaven. I do not fear prison or death.

Recently, one of our missionaries in Africa was sacrificed. When I hear such reports, what do I think? 'You have walked your path.' I think, 'You will become the ancestor of the Unification Church in that country.' That is what I think. 'If you had died for the world like Reverend Moon, you would become the ancestor of the world.' I am walking that path now. For that, without even worrying about it, he lived a more public life than anyone else.

You must walk the path of love for God and the universe.

Look, when there is a nation in the world, that nation is protected. You need to understand that. Why do we need to do such things? Why do we need the world and heaven? If there is heaven, heaven protects the world. Therefore, the world is needed, and heaven is needed. This is the same principle. If there had been no fall, it would have been automatically protected, but this has been broken. (Writing on the board while speaking) If you erase all this, such a line will be drawn. If there had been no fall, this would have become a straight protective line, all of it. What this means is that it means protection 24 hours a day.

Now, if I connect with heaven, what happens? Heaven arises outside of me. It connects to this world. Because of the fall, it has become a different world. Therefore, to connect with heaven, we must overcome this. We must cross this boundary line. Even in the spirit world, now, being soaked in the chaotic fallen atmosphere, you must think that you are within the boundary of the fallen nature. It is the same. Therefore, if there are people in the spirit world, they are trying to get out. There are countless forms. There are many ranks, and they are all different, so they are trying to get out. Therefore, we must cross this line, this boundary. It is all the same.

So in the end, at this time... When there is a boundary, when viewed from the center of this boundary line, it is not straight like this. It all tries to spread in all directions. Here, it tries to go this way, and here it tries to go that way, and it is all like that. This is different. Originally, they should all come together and go like this (in a straight line). (Writing on the board while speaking) The spirit world is like this. But because we cannot see this, chaos ensues.

Since we have walked the path of the fall, we must teach the path that must be taken from here. In the spirit world, they are trying to find their way in reverse. When they find their way in the spirit world, they are trying to come in from here in reverse. Only then can the spirit world be connected with the earthly world. (Writing on the board while speaking)

Now, would God want that, or would humans want that? They all do not want it. That is why the spiritual world connecting with the human world and touching it to create a new revival happens only once every few centuries or hundreds of years, once every few centuries. How much effort has been made for the spirit world and the human world to unite and break through? But until now, it has not been resolved. Do you understand what I mean?

Do you think that receiving such grace in the Unification Church and experiencing such spiritual experiences is cheap? You must understand that since the fall of humanity, God has paid the price of all sacrifices to pour the core essence into this place. Therefore, when you cannot take responsibility, you must be judged based on historical conditions of accusation. Do you understand what I mean?

In the Unification Church, now in the era of Reverend Moon, we are taught to go from the individual to the family, tribe, and nation... This is how we are taught to go. Therefore, there are two paths to enter this world, but if the individual sacrifices for the tribe, that individual is transferred into the tribal realm. That is how it becomes a straight line. Do you understand what I mean? What is the Unification Church of today working for? It is working for the world. It has come in to work for the world.

Now is the time to fight to restore the world and the spirit world. 

Here, the American people, the leaders of America, must sacrifice for the world, not for America. If they sacrifice for the world, what happens? A nation is born, a nation. A nation will arise here. You will see a nation arise. Do you understand what I mean? 「Yes」

Then this house is a house for the nation. The house of love is the same. Reverend Moon's hair resembles Reverend Moon. It is the same. It resembles me. All elements are the same.

That is why in terms of vitality, everything is connected. The individual is connected by vitality, and the universe is connected by love; you must understand this. You must understand this. Eating rice, eating for life is indeed the truth. Loving rice is the truth. That is the truth. What is the truth? It is eternal. Every human must eat rice eternally. Eating is the truth, and that truth is eternal. Love is the truth, and truth is eternal. That is not only for me; our ancestors also must seek love, and for thousands of years, humans must seek love. That is the truth. Eating is truth, loving between husband and wife is truth, and giving birth to children is truth.

So no matter how hard it is for a woman, I hope she gives birth. Look when she turns 30 or 40. She says, 'Oh, even if my legs are torn apart, I will give birth once.' Young girls, when asked to get married, initially say, 'Oh, I am scared of giving birth, I cannot go.' They do not know. When they turn 30 or 40, they say, 'Oh, if I cannot give birth...' They think that way and have that concept. That thought will be accepted everywhere. Do you understand what I mean? 「Yes」

So in our Unification Church, let us work for the world and the spirit world! 「Yes」 After the world becomes one, the spirits in hell will say, 'Oh, I wish that stepping stone on the ground would be removed!' They will want it removed. That must be eliminated. That New Yorker hotel...

You cannot get out even if you want to. Who will remove this? So, you have no choice but to come down to the earth, and keep coming back... The Unification Church's anti-communist movement is for the country and the world.
 Now, do you think Reverend Moon is doing this because he is inferior to you? If there were no spirit world, I wouldn't be doing this. Even if I were told to do it, I wouldn't. Because I know the spirit world... 
If I don't do it, it will be a big problem. It will be a disaster. The country is in chaos and the world is in chaos, so I have no choice... If you break, you break, but I will not break. Is there anything like this in the era of Reverend Moon? "No." Is there ever going to be a time like this in the Unification Church's era of Reverend Moon? It seems like that time has passed, does it seem like it will come again?

Reagan is in the position of rebuilding conservative Christian thought and traditional thought to defeat communism. Carter helped the communists. He cannot be anti-communist. KAFP, you should be at the forefront.' The American people know nothing. Reagan doesn't know, and the American administration doesn't know. As soon as the presidential inauguration is over, the communists will demonstrate nationwide. They will run rampant in the country, nationwide. Look, that's how it will be. The Reagan administration is being directed by Reverend Moon in ways they never even considered. We are making full preparations.

The Two Worlds of Good and Evil

Even the people sitting here, if I say, "You are evil people," they get offended, and conversely, if I say, "Oh, you are good people. You are good," they respond with "Hmm!" (Showing expressions) Generally, people like good, but they don't know well about the criteria of good and evil. Where is the boundary between good and evil? 

In this world, good and evil coexist. 

Now, if you look at yourselves, everything is made up of the two worlds of good and evil. There are eyes of the good world and eyes of the evil world, noses of the good world and noses of the evil world, ears, hands, bodies, and all aspects of life are divided into two. Families can be good families or evil families, politics can be good politics or evil politics, and what we eat can also be good or evil. Everything is like that. And there are good countries and bad countries, good laws and bad laws, good thoughts and bad thoughts... everything is like that. 

So, if we want to be good people, we must eat only good food, breathe only good air, see only good things, and feel only good feelings. We can conclude that feeling, living, and everything in that country must be in a good environment to be a good person; otherwise, everything is evil. 

If there is an apple here, even if it looks good and tastes delicious, if it has a disease, it becomes a bad apple because of that. (Drawing a picture while speaking) If it has even a little bit of disease, it is absolutely not good. It cannot be treated as good. There is no possibility of being regarded as good. That is the truth. Therefore, outside of the criteria of good, everything other than perfect good is evil. Then, what is good? It is something that everyone likes, hopes for, loves, and can encompass everything. 

Now, Americans say, "America is a good country." In this light, is America a good country? Now, if a person likes alcohol, in other words, an alcoholic, they say, "Oh, alcohol is good," while ordinary people say, "Alcohol is bad." When it comes to eating, if one eats according to their portion, that food is good, but if they eat too much, even good food becomes bad food. We are all like that. Even in sleeping, there are people who sleep badly... 

When you look at your home, if there are five family members living together, are all five of them good people? Who among the mother, father, and siblings is truly a good person? Is it the mother, the father, or the siblings? This is the problem. Therefore, there must be principles in how to distinguish good and evil. 

The two worlds of good and evil start from two people.

That good must be perfect. It must be complete. To be good, everything must be perfect. When we look at a person, even if all limbs are healthy, if our brain is slightly wrong, everything...
